### Exam: aqua-rat-100 | Temperature: 1.0 | Problem 97 of 100 ###
Topic: Math
Question: An organization decided to raise Rs. 6 lakh by collecting equal contribution from each of its employees. If each of them had contributed Rs. 60 extra, the contribution would have been Rs. 6.24 lakh. How many employees are there in that organization?
Choices:
  A: 300
  B: 200
  C: 400
  D: 100
  E: 500
Response 0:
Let's assume that there are 'n' employees in the organization and each employee contributes 'x' amount of money. 

So, the total amount collected by 'n' employees is n*x. 

According to the question, 
n*x = 6,00,000  ----(1) 

If each employee had contributed Rs. 60 extra, then the new contribution per employee would be (x+60) and the total contribution would be 6,24,000. 

So, the new equation would be:
n*(x+60) = 6,24,000  ----(2)

We need to find the value of 'n'. 

Let's solve the above two equations to get the value of 'n'. 

n*x = 6,00,000  ----(1) 
n*(x+60) = 6,24,000  ----(2)

Expanding equation (2), we get:
n*x + 60n = 6,24,000

Substituting the value of n*x from equation (1), we get:
6,00,000 + 60n = 6,24,000

Simplifying the above equation, we get:
60n = 24,000
n = 400

Therefore, there are 400 employees in the organization.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 1:
Let's assume that there are 'n' employees in the organization and each employee contributes 'x' amount of money. 

So, the total amount collected by 'n' employees is given as:
nx = 6,00,000  ----(1)

Now, if each employee contributes Rs. 60 extra, the new contribution per employee becomes (x+60). So, the new total amount collected by 'n' employees is given as:
n(x+60) = 6,24,000

Expanding the above equation, we get:
nx + 60n = 6,24,000

Substituting the value of nx from equation (1), we get:
6,00,000 + 60n = 6,24,000

Solving for 'n', we get:
n = 400

Therefore, there are 400 employees in the organization.
Action: Answer("C")
Response 2:
Let's assume that there are "x" employees in the organization. 

Knowledge:
  If each employee contributes "y" amount, then the total contribution would be x*y.
  According to the problem, the total contribution is Rs. 6 lakh when each employee contributes equally.
  If each employee contributes Rs. 60 extra, then the new contribution from each employee would be (y+60).
  The new total contribution would be x*(y+60) = Rs. 6.24 lakh.

Calculation:
  From the above equations, we can write:
  xy = 6,00,000
  x(y+60) = 6,24,000

  By solving these equations, we get:
  xy + 60x = 6,24,000
  6,00,000 + 60x = 6,24,000
  60x = 24,000
  x = 400

Action: Answer("C")

Topic: Math
Question: A man divides Rs 8600 among 5 sons, 4 daughters and 2 nephews. If each daughter receives four times as much as each nephew, and each son receives five as much as each nephew. How much does each daughter receive ?
Choices:
  A: Rs 400
  B: Rs 500
  C: Rs 600
  D: Rs 700
  E: Rs 800
Response 0:
Let the amount received by each nephew be x.
Then, each daughter receives 4x and each son receives 5x.
The total number of recipients is 5+4+2 = 11.
Therefore, we have the equation:
5(5x) + 4(4x) + 2(x) = 8600
Simplifying this equation, we get:
33x = 8600
x = 260
Therefore, each daughter receives 4x = 4(260) = 1040.
Action: Answer("A")

Question: A student instead of finding the value of 7/8 of a number, found the value of 7/18 of the number. If his answer differed from the actual one by 770, find the that number.
Choices:
  A: 1584
  B: 2520
  C: 1728
  D: 1656
  E: None
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  Let the number be x.

Question: Calculate the maximum distance you can travel with $8.50 on a cab which charges $3.50 for the first quarter-mile and 10 cents for each additional quarter mile.
Choices:
  A: 11.75 miles
  B: 12.75 miles
  C: 17.75 miles
  D: 14.75 miles
  E: 10.75 miles
Response 0:
Knowledge:
  The cab charges $3.50 for the first quarter-mile and 10 cents for each additional quarter mile.
  We need to find the maximum distance that can be traveled with $8.50.
  To solve this problem, we can use the formula: distance = (amount paid - fixed charge) / variable charge
  The fixed charge is $3.50 and the variable charge is $0.10 per quarter mile.

Action: 
  First, we need to subtract the fixed charge from the amount paid: $8.50 - $3.50 = $5.00
  Then, we need to divide the remaining amount by the variable charge: $5.00 / $0.10 per quarter mile = 50 quarter miles
  Therefore, the maximum distance that can be traveled is 50 quarter miles, which is equal to 12.5 miles.
  However, we need to subtract the first quarter mile, which was already paid for: 12.5 miles - 0.25 miles = 12.25 miles.
  Answer: Answer("D")
